           <input @blur="onCompanySearchBlur()" @focus="getCompanies()" autocomplete="off" class="form-control ps-2xl pe-lg" id="companySearchInput" name="companySearch" placeholder="Find Company" type="text" x-model="companySearchTerm" x-on:input.debounce="getCompanies()" x-on:keydown.arrow-down.prevent="nextCompany()" x-on:keydown.arrow-up.prevent="previousCompany()" x-on:keyup.enter="selectCompany(selectedCompanyIndex &gt;= 0 ? availableCompanyOptions[selectedCompanyIndex] : null)" x-ref="companySearchInput"/>
           <i class="fa-solid fa-magnifying-glass fs-lg company-search-input-icon">
           </i>
           <label class="company-search-label" for="companySearchInput">
            Find Company
           </label>
          </div>
          <ul class="dropdown-menu p-0 w-100">
           <div class="list-group">
            <template x-if="availableCompanyOptions.length &gt; 0">
             <template :key="company.id" x-for="(company,index) in availableCompanyOptions">
              <label :class="{'active' : index === selectedCompanyIndex}" class="list-group-item list-group-item-action text-truncate" x-on:click.stop="selectCompany(company)">
               <div :id="'company-' + company.id" type="button" x-text="company.title">
               </div>
              </label>
             </template>
            </template>
            <template x-if="availableCompanyOptions.length === 0 &amp;&amp; companySearchTerm.length &gt; 0">
             <div class="list-group-item text-nowrap">
              No Results Found
             </div>
            </template>
           </div>
          </ul>
         </div>
        </div>
       </div>
       <div class="mb-md pb-lg" id="companySize-offcanvas">
        <div :class="{'bg-gray-01-highlight rounded-3 d-flex w-100 align-content-center' : selectedCompanySizeAliases.length &gt; 0}" class="font-barlow fw-medium fs-xl mb-md p-sm">
         Company Size
         <i class="ms-auto fa-solid fa-check text-primary fs-2xl" x-show="selectedCompanySizeAliases.length &gt; 0">
         </i>

           <span class="form-check-label text-nowrap" x-text="companySize.name">
           </span>
          </label>
